 chunavi hinsa or khun kharabe ke liye charchit hue pashchim bengal main panchayat chunaav ke nattejey 17 may ko ghoshit ho gaye
 The violence during these elections in Bengal killed at least 14 people and injured a large number of people
 chunaav ke dauraan hui hinsa kii kai tasviren or kai dil dahala dene walevideosamne aae, lekin ek video aisa aayaa jise dekhakar logon ne daanton tale ungali dabaa lee
 Everyone would have heard about the booth capturing, but seeing the way the open booth is being looted in this viral video, it is difficult to believe that any such election can happen
 ballat paper se hue panchayat chunaavaap khud dekhie isvideoko jisko lekar soshal media main behad halchal he
 The panchayat elections in West Bengal were not evms but ballot papers
 yah video is kadar viral hua ki ise chunaav main dhaandhlee kii misaal kaha jane laga
 We decided to find out the truth of this very popular video
 video dekhte hi saaf ho jaataa he ki ye video pashchim bengal chunaav kaa he
 The election trail of BJP, Trinamool Congress, CPM and Congress Party can be clearly seen on the ballot paper
 safed shart vaala aadmi jis samay kai ballat paper par trinmul congress ke chunaav nishaan par muhar lagaakar ballat box main daal rahaa he us samay ye bhi dekha ja saktaa he ki saamne bangla or angreji main matdaan kaksh likhaa hua he
 The Bengal Panchayat election is being done on the video ballot papers, it is yellow in color
 saath main kinare rakhe hue gulabi rang ke duusare bailat paper bhi dikh rahe hai
 This time in the Bengal Panchayat elections, the color of the ballot paper of the Zilla Parishad election was yellow and the color of the ballot paper of the Panchayat Samiti was pink
 in baton se ye to saaf ho gaya ki ye video bengal panchayat chunaavon kaa hi he
 The next challenge was to find out whether this video is for this election and if yes then, which place, which seat and booth is this
 video main dhyaan se sunne se pataa chalata he ki jo vyakti gaiyrkanoonee tareeke se bailat paper par muhar lagaataa chalaa ja rahaa he uske alaava bhi vahaan kam se kam do-teen or log maujuud hai
 These people are taking pictures and making videos
 bangla main ho rahi baatcheet main video banane vaala vyakti use bharosa dilaane kii koshish kar rahaa he ki uskaa cheharaa nahin dikhegaa
 Sometimes the glimpse of people engaged in making videos and taking photos is also seen in the video
 ek baar ek profeshnal camere kaa lens bhi frem main dikhataa he
 That is, when this was happening, maybe some media people were also present there
 14 may ko hui thi votingis baat kaa pataa lagane ke liye jab hamane bangla ke kuch sthaneey tivi channels or akhabaaron main sampark kiya to ye pataa chalaa ki ye ghatana uttari 24 pargana jile kii he jahaan 14 may ko voting hui thi
 We also had a conversation with a man who, on the condition of anonymity, told us that he was present at the time when this feat was happening
 uske daawey ke mutabik ye ghatana kolkata ke paas rajarhat tehsil main hui thi
 It was also learned that a booth in Patharghata village of Rajarhat was captured on May 14 in this way and these pictures may be there
 kai sthaneey logon ke baat karke pataa chalaa ki ye booth number 204 ki ghatana he jahaan ek shishu shiksha centre ko poling booth banaaya gaya tha
 But instead of directly believing this claim, we started trying to find out whether it is really a polling station in Patharghata
 video main dekha ja saktaa he ki ballat paper par pehle number par bijepi, duusare number par trinmul, tisare number par sipiem or chauthe number par congress kaa chunaav nishaan chapa he
 That is, four candidates were in the fray for this seat
 4 partiyon ke ummidavaarpata chalaa ki patharghata seat number 33 par inhen chaar partiyon ke ummidavaar maidan main he
 In this matter, we have found out what are the rules for writing the names of parties or candidates on the ballot paper
 chunaav se jude adhikariyon ne bataaya ki ballat paper par partiyon or ummidavaaron kaa faisla, elfabetical order main likhaa jaataa he , lekin bangla bhashaa ke varnmaala ke hisaab se
 We extracted the list of candidates for the Zilla Parishad election at Patharghata seat number 33
 bijepi ke ummidavaar kaa naam achint kumaar naskar, trinmul ke ummidavaar kaa naam gaur naskar, sipiem ke ummidavaar kaa naam baapi biswas or congress ke ummidavaar kaa naam ratna bhattacharya he
 According to Bangla language, these names will come in the same order as printed on this ballot paper i
